### <a id="inductive-types-h-s-p-and-v">Inductive Types H, S, P, and V</a>

This section presents the [UALib.Varieties.Varieties][] module of the [Agda Universal Algebra Library][].

Fix a signature 𝑆, let 𝒦 be a class of 𝑆-algebras, and define

* H 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a homomorphic image of a members of 𝒦;
* S 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a subalgebra of a member of 𝒦;
* P 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a product of members of 𝒦.

A straight-forward verification confirms that H, S, and P are **closure operators** (expansive, monotone, and idempotent).  A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is said to be *closed under the taking of homomorphic images* provided `H 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. Similarly, 𝒦 is *closed under the taking of subalgebras* (resp., *arbitrary products*) provided `S 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦` (resp., `P 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`).

An algebra is a homomorphic image (resp., subalgebra; resp., product) of every algebra to which it is isomorphic. Thus, the class `H 𝒦` (resp., `S 𝒦`; resp., `P 𝒦`) is closed under isomorphism.

The operators H, S, and P can be composed with one another repeatedly, forming yet more closure operators.

<!-- If C₁ and C₂ are closure operators on classes of structures, let us say that C₁ ≤ C₂ if for every class 𝒦 we have C₁(𝒦) ⊆ C₂(𝒦). -->

A **variety** is a class 𝒦 of algebras in a fixed signature that is closed under the taking of homomorphic images (H), subalgebras (S), and arbitrary products (P).  That is, 𝒦 is a variety if and only if `H S P 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`.

This module defines what we have found to be the most useful inductive types representing the closure operators H, S, and P. Separately, we define the inductive type `V` for simultaneously representing closure under `H`, `S`, and `P`.

<!-- ; consequently, we expect `V 𝒦 ≡ H (S (P 𝒦))` to hold for each class 𝒦 of algebras of a fixed signature. classes of algebras that are closed under H, S, P, and V ≡ HSP. -->

#### <a id="homomorphic-closure">Homomorphism closure</a>

We define the inductive type `H` to represent classes of algebras that include all homomorphic images of algebras in the class; i.e., classes that are closed under the taking of homomorphic images.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="2755" class="Comment">--Closure wrt H</a>

  <a id="H.hiso"></a><a id="3073" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3073" class="InductiveConstructor">hiso</a>  <a id="3079" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3081" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3082" <!-- We say that a class 𝒦 is **closed under** `H` (or `H`-**closed**) provided `H 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. -->

--------------------------------

#### <a id="subalgebra-closure">Subalgebra closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing classes of algebras that are closed under the taking of subalgebras as an inductive type.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="3521" class="Comment">--Closure wrt S</a>
<a id="3537" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="S"></a><a id="3542" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3542" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="3544" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3545" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3545" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3547" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3547" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="3549" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3551" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="3559" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="3561" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3561" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="3563" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3565" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="3570" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3571" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3579" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3545" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3581" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3582" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3584" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3585" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="3588" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3545" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="3589" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="3592" class="Symbol">:</a>
 <a id="3595" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="3600" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3601" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3609" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3610" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3545" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3612" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="3614" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3547" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="3615" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3617" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3618" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3620" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3621" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="3624" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3625" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3545" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3627" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="3629" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3547" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="3630" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="3633" class="Keyword">where</a>

href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3561" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>

<!-- A class 𝒦 is **closed under** `S` (or `S`-**closed**) provided `S 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦` -->

-----------------------------------------

#### <a id="product-closure">Product closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing classes of algebras closed under arbitrary products is the following. 

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="4325" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="P"></a><a id="4330" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4330" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4332" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4333" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4333" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4335" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4335" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="4337" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4339" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="4347" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4349" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4350" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4350" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4352" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4354" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="4359" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4360" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4368" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4333" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4370" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4371" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4373" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4374" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="4377" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4333" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4378" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="4381" class="Symbol">:</a>
 <a id="4384" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="4389" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4390" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4398" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4399" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4333" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4401" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="4403" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4335" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4404" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4406" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4407" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4409" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4410" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="4413" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4414" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4333" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4416" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="4418" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4335" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4419" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="4422" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="P.pbase"></a><a id="4430" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4430" class="InductiveConstructor">pbase</a>  <a id="4437" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4439" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4440" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4440" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4442" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4444" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4452" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4333" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4454" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4455" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4457" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4459" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4440" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4461" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4463" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4350" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4465" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4467" href="UALib.Algebras.Lifts.html#3828" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="4476" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4440" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4478" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4335" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="4480" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4482" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4330" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4484" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4350" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

  <a id="P.prodw"></a><a id="4715" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4715" class="InductiveConstructor">prodw</a>  <a id="4722" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4724" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4725" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4779" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4781" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4350" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="4782" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4784" class="Symbol">→</a> <a class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="4864" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4825" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4866" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4868" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4825" </pre>

<!-- A class 𝒦 is **closed under** `P` (or `P`-**closed**) provided `P 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. -->

-----------------------------------------------

#### <a id="variety-closure">Varietal closure</a>

A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is called a **variety** if it is closed under each of the closure operators H, S, and P introduced above; the corresponding closure operator is often denoted 𝕍, but we will typically denote it by `V`.

Thus, if 𝒦 is a class of 𝑆-algebras, then the **variety generated by** 𝒦 is denoted by `V 𝒦` and defined to be the smallest class that contains 𝒦 and is closed under `H`, `S`, and `P`.

We now define `V` as an inductive type.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="5605" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="V"></a><a id="5610" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5610" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5612" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5613" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5613" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5615" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5615" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="5617" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5619" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="5627" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="5629" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5629" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5631" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5633" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5638" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5639" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5647" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5613" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5649" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5650" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5652" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5653" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="5656" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5613" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5657" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5660" class="Symbol">:</a>
 <a id="5663" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5668" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5669" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5677" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5678" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5613" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5680" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="5682" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5615" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5683" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5685" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5686" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="5688" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="5691" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5692" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5613" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5694" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="5696" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5615" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5697" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5700" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="V.vbase"></a><a id="5708" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5708" class="InductiveConstructor">vbase</a>  <a id="5715" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5717" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5718" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5718" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5720" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5722" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5730" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5613" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5732" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5733" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5735" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5737" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5718" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5739" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5741" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5629" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5743" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5745" href="UALib.Algebras.Lifts.html#3828" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="5754" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5718" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5756" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5615" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="5758" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5760" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5610" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5762" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5629" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

-------------------------------

#### <a id="closure-properties">Closure properties</a>

The types defined above represent operators with useful closure properties. We now prove a handful of such properties since we will need them later.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="6701" class="Comment">-- P is a closure operator; in particular, it&#39;s expansive.</a>
<a id="P-expa"></a><a id="6760" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6760" class="Function">P-expa</a> <a id="6767" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6769" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6770" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6770" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6772" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6774" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="6782" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6784" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6784" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="6786" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6788" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="6793" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6794" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="6802" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6770" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6804" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="6805" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="6807" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="6810" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6770" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6811" class="Symbol">)}</a>
 <a id="6815" class="Symbol">→</a>       <a id="6823" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6784" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="6825" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2949" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="6827" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4330" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="6828" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6829" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6770" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6830" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6832" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6770" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6833" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6835" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6784" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

<a id="6838" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6760" class="Function">P-expa</a><a id="6844" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6845" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6845" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6846" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6848" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6848" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="6849" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6851" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6852" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6852" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="6853" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6855" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6855" class="Bound">KA</a> <a id="6858" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6860" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4798" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a><a id="6865" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6866" class="Argument">𝑨</a> <a id="6868" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6870" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6871" href="UALib.Algebras.Lifts.html#3828" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="6880" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6852" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="6882" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6845" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6883" class="Symbol">)}{</a><a id="6886" class="Argument">𝑩</a> <a id="6888" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6890" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6852" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="6891" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6893" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6894" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4430" class="InductiveConstructor">pbase</a> <a id="6900" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6855" class="Bound">KA</a><a id="6902" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6904" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6905" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2380" class="Function">sym-≅</a> <a id="6911" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4327" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="6921" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="6924" class="Comment">-- P is a closure operator; in particular, it&#39;s idempotent.</a>

<a id="7485" class="Comment">-- S is a closure operator; in particular, it&#39;s monotone.</a>

<a id="7885" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7543" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7892" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7892" class="Bound">ante</a> <a id="7897" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7898" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3906" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="7903" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7903" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7905" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7905" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="7907" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7909" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7911" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3906" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="7916" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7917" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7543" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7924" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7892" class="Bound">ante</a> <a id="7929" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7903" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7930" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7932" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7905" class="Bound">x₁</a>

</pre>

We sometimes want to go back and forth between our two representations of subalgebras of algebras in a class. The tools `subalgebra→S` and `S→subalgebra` are made for that purpose.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="subalgebra→S"></a><a id="8144" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8144" class="Function">subalgebra→S</a> <a id="8157" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8159" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8160" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8160" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8162" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8162" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="8164" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8166" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="8174" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="8176" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8176" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="8178" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8180" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="8185" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8186" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="8194" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8160" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8196" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="8197" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="8199" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="8202" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8160" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="8203" class="Symbol">)}</a>
               <a id="8221" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8222" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8222" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="8224" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8226" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="8234" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8235" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8160" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8237" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="8239" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8162" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="8240" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8242" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="8243" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8245" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8247" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8222" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="8249" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2536" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="8269" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8176" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
             <a id="8284" class="Comment">----------------------------------------------------------</a>

  <a id="9901" class="Keyword">where</a>
   <a id="9910" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9910" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="9913" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9915" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9884" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="9917" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2536" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="9937" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8631" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

   <a id="10011" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10011" class="Function">A≅SA</a> <a id="10016" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10018" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9884" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="10020" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#861" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="10022" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="10024" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9966" class="Function">SA</a> <a id="10027" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a>
   <a id="10032" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10011" class="Function">A≅SA</a> <a id="10037" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10039" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10456" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="10043" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10452" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="10045" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10456" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="10049" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9910" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="10052" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10452" class="Function Operator">∥</a>

</pre>

Next we observe that lifting to a higher universe does not break the property of being a subalgebra of an algebra of a class.  In other words, if we lift a subalgebra of an algebra in a class, the result is still a subalgebra of an algebra in the class.

<pre class="Agda">

The next lemma would be too obvoius to care about were it not for the fact that we'll need it later, so it too must be formalized.

<pre class="Agda">

  <a id="12961" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12961" class="Function">lA≅B</a> <a id="12966" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12968" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12651" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="12971" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#861" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="12973" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12591" class="Bound">𝑩</a>
  <a id="12977" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12961" class="Function">lA≅B</a> <a id="12982" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12984" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3811" class="Function">Trans-≅</a> <a id="12992" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12651" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="12995" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12591" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="12997" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12998" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2380" class="Function">sym-≅</a> <a id="13004" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4327" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="13014" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13016" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12606" class="Bound">A≅B</a>

</pre>

We need to formalize one more lemma before arriving the short term objective of this section, which is the proof of the inclusion PS⊆SP.

<pre class="Agda">

class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="14106" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14108" class="Argument">𝓘</a> <a id="14110" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14112" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13461" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="14113" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14115" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13467" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="14119" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13467"     <a id="14161" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14161" class="Function">iii</a> <a id="14165" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14167" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Basic.html#2093" class="Function">is-homomorphism</a> <a id="14183" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14184" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="14186" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13569" class="Function">SA</a><a id="14188" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14190" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14191" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="14193" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13524" class="Function">𝒜</a><a id="14194" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14196" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13995" class="Function">i</a>
    <a id="14202" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14161" class="Function">iii</a> <a id="14206" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14208" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="14210" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14210" class="Bound">𝑓</a> <a id="14212" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14212" class="Bound">𝒂</a> <a id="14214" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14216" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2277" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="14220" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="14222" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14222" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="14224" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14226" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14227" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10456" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="14231" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10452" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="14233" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13806" class="Function">SA≤𝒜</a> <a id="14238" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14222" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="14240" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10452" class="Function Operator">∥</a><a id="14241" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14243" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14210" class="Bound">𝑓</a> <a id="14245" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="14248" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14248" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14250" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14252" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14212" class="Bound">𝒂</a> <a id="14254" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14248" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14256" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14222" class="Bound">i</a><a id="14257" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="14262" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14262" class="Function">ξ</a> <a id="14264" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14266" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="14268" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13524" class="Function">𝒜</a> <a id="14270" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="14272" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4330" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="14274" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13464" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
  <a id="14278" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14262" class="Function">ξ</a> <a id="14280" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14282" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4632" class="InductiveConstructor">produ</a><a id="14287" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14288" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13458" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="14289" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14291" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13461" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="14292" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14294" class="Argument">I</a> <a id="14296" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14298" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13472" class="Bound">I</a><a id="14299" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14301" class="Argument">𝒜</a> <a id="14303" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14305" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13524" class="Function">𝒜</a><a id="14306" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14308" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="14311" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14311" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="14313" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14315" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6760" class="Function">P-expa</a> <a id="14322" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14323" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13624" class="Function">KA</a> <a id="14326" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14311" class="Bound">i</a><a id="14327" class="Symbol">))</a>

  <a id="14333" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14333" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="14335" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14337" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="14339" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13475" class="Bound">ℬ</a> <a id="14341" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#861" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="14343" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="14345" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13569" class="Function">SA</a>
  <a id="14350" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14333" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="14352" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14354" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#6161" class="Function">⨅≅</a> <a id="14357" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2277" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="14361" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13677" class="Function">B≅SA</a>

</pre>

#### PS(𝒦) ⊆ SP(𝒦)

Finally, we are in a position to prove that a product of subalgebras of algebras in a class 𝒦 is a subalgebra of a product of algebras in 𝒦.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="14555" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="14562" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14562" class="Module">_</a> <a id="14564" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14565" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14565" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="14567" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14569" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="14577" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14579" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14579" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="14581" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14583" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="14588" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14589" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="14597" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14565" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="14599" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="14600" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="14602" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="14605" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14565" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="14606" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="14609" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14610" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14610" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="14614" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14616" href="MGS-FunExt-from-Univalence.html#2235" class="Function">hfunext</a> <a id="14624" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14625" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="14628" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14565" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="14629" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="14631" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="14634" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14565" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="14635" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="14638" class="Keyword">where</a>

#### <a id="more-class-inclusions">More class inclusions</a>

We conclude this module with three more inclusion relations that will have bit parts to play in our formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem.

<a id="16869" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16598" class="Function">P⊆V</a> <a id="16873" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16874" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4798" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a> <a id="16880" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16880" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="16882" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16882" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="16884" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16886" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16888" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6292" class="InductiveConstructor">visou</a> <a id="16894" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16895" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16598" class="Function">P⊆V</a> <a id="16899" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16880" class="Bound">x</a><a id="16900" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16902" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16882" class="Bound">x₁</a>

<a id="SP⊆V"></a><a id="16942" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16942" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="16947" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16949" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16950" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16950" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="16952" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16952" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="16954" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16956" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="16964" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16966" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16966" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="16968" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16970" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="16975" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16976" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="16984" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16950" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="16986" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="16987" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="16989" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="16992" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16950" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16993" class="Symbol">)}</a>
 <a id="16997" class="Symbol">→</a>    <a id="17002" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3542" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="17003" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17004" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16950" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17006" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="17008" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16952" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="17009" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17011" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16950" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17013" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="17015" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16952" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="17016" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17018" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17019" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4330" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="17020" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17021" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16950" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17022" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17024" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16952" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="17025" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17027" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16966" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="17028" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17030" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2949" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="17032" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5610" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="17033" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17034" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16950" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17035" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17037" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16952" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="17038" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17040" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16966" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
<a id="17042" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16942" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17047" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17048" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3641" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a><a id="17053" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17054" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17054" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="17055" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17057" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17057" class="Bound">PCloA</a><a id="17062" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17064" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17066" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16598" class="Function">P⊆V</a> <a id="17070" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17071" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4878" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a> <a id="17077" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17057" class="Bound">PCloA</a> <a id="17083" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4327" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="17093" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="17095" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16942" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17100" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17101" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3698" class="InductiveConstructor">slift</a><a id="17106" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17107" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17107" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="17108" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17110" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17110" class="Bound">x</a><a id="17111" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17113" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17115" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5832" class="InductiveConstructor">vliftw</a> <a id="17122" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17123" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16942" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17128" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17110" class="Bound">x</a><a id="17129" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="17252" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16942" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17257" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17258" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3906" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="17263" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17263" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="17265" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17265" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="17267" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17269" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17271" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6372" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="17277" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17278" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16942" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17283" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17263" class="Bound">x</a><a id="17284" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17286" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17265" class="Bound">x₁</a>

</pre>


#### <a id="products-of-classes">Products of classes</a>

Above we proved PS(𝒦) ⊆ SP(𝒦).  It is slightly more painful to prove that the product of *all* algebras in the class S(𝒦) is a member of SP(𝒦). That is, ⨅ S(𝒦) ∈ SP(𝒦). This is mainly due to the fact that it's not obvious (at least not to this author-coder) what should be the type of the product of all members of a class of algebras.  After a few false starts, eventually the right type revealed itself.  Of course, now that we have it in our hands, it seems rather obvious.

We now describe the this type of product of all algebras in an arbitrary class 𝒦 of algebras of the same signature.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="17970" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="class-product"></a><a id="17977" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17977" class="Module">class-product</a> <a id="17991" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17992" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17992" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17994" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17996" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="18004" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18006" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18006" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="18008" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18010" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="18015" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18016" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18024" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17992" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18026" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18027" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18029" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18030" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="18033" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17992" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18034" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="18037" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="18045" class="Comment">-- ℑ serves as an index for the class</a>
 <a id="class-product.ℑ"></a><a id="18084" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18084" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="18086" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18088" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18089" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18089" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18091" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18093" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="18101" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18103" class="Symbol">→</a>  <a id="18106" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="18111" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18112" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18120" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18089" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18122" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18123" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="18125" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="18128" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18089" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18129" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18131" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18133" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18134" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="18137" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18089" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18138" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18140" href="universes.html#758" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
 <a id="18143" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18084" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="18145" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18146" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18146" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18147" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18149" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18149" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="18151" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18153" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="18155" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18155" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18157" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="18159" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18160" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18168" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18146" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18170" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18171" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18173" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">,</a> <a id="18175" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18155" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18177" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="18179" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18149" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

  <a id="18184" class="Comment">-- 𝔄 produces an algebra for each index (i : ℑ).</a>
 <a id="class-product.𝔄"></a><a id="18234" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18234" class="Function">𝔄</a> <a id="18236" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18238" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18239" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18239" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18241" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18243" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="18251" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18253" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18253" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="18255" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18257" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="18262" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18263" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18271" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18239" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18273" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18274" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="18276" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="18279" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18239" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18280" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="18283" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18285" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18084" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="18287" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18253" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="18289" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18291" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18299" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18239" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18301" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
 <a id="18304" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18234" class="Function">𝔄</a><a id="18305" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18306" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18306" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18307" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18309" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18309" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="18310" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18312" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18314" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="18316" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18317" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18317" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="18319" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18321" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18322" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18084" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="18324" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18309" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="18325" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="18328" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18330" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="18332" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18317" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="18334" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a>

 <a id="18338" class="Comment">-- The product of all members of 𝒦 can be written simply as follows:</a>
 <a id="class-product.class-product"></a><a id="18408" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18408" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="18422" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18424" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18425" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18425" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18427" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18429" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="18437" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18439" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18441" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="18446" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18447" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18455" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18425" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18457" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18458" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="18460" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="18463" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18425" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18464" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18466" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18468" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18476" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18477" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="18480" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18425" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18481" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18483" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
 <a id="18486" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18408" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="18500" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18501" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18501" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18502" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18504" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18504" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="18506" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18508" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="18510" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18512" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18234" class="Function">𝔄</a><a id="18513" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18514" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18501" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18515" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18517" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18504" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="18518" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18520" class="Symbol">)</a>

 <a id="18524" class="Comment">-- ...or, more explicitly, here is the expansion of this indexed product.</a>
 <a id="class-product.class-product&#39;"></a><a id="18599" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18599" class="Function">class-product&#39;</a> <a id="18614" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18616" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18617" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18617" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18619" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18621" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="18629" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18631" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18633" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="18638" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18639" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18647" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18617" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18649" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18650" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="18652" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="18655" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18617" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18656" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18658" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18660" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18668" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18669" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="18672" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18617" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18673" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18675" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
 <a id="18678" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18599" class="Function">class-product&#39;</a><a id="18692" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18693" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18693" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18694" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18696" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18696" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="18698" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18700" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="18702" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="18704" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18705" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18705" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="18707" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18709" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18710" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="18712" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18712" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18714" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="18716" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18717" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18725" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18693" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18727" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18728" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18730" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">,</a> <a id="18732" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18712" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18734" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="18736" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18696" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="18737" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="18740" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18742" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="18744" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18705" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="18746" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a>

</pre>

Notice that, if `p : 𝑨 ∈ 𝒦`, then we can think of the pair `(𝑨 , p) ∈ ℑ 𝒦` as an index over the class, and so we can think of `𝔄 (𝑨 , p)` (which is obviously `𝑨`) as the projection of the product `⨅ ( 𝔄{𝓤}{𝒦} )` onto the `(𝑨 , p)`-th component.

#### ⨅ S(𝒦) ∈ SP(𝒦)
Finally, we prove the result that plays a leading role in the formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem---namely, that our newly defined class product ⨅ ( 𝔄{𝓤}{𝒦} ) belongs to SP(𝒦).

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="19218" class="Comment">-- The product of all subalgebras of a class 𝒦 belongs to SP(𝒦).</a>
<a id="19283" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="class-product-inclusions"></a><a id="19290" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19290" class="Module">class-product-inclusions</a> <a id="19315" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19316" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19316" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19318" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19320" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="19328" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19330" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19331" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19331" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="19333" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19335" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="19340" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19341" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19349" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19316" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19351" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="19352" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="19354" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="19357" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19316" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19358" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="19361" class="Keyword">where</a>

   <a id="19847" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19847" class="Function">psPllA</a> <a id="19854" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19856" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="19858" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19593" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="19862" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="19864" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4330" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="19866" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19867" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3542" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="19869" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19331" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19870" class="Symbol">)</a>
   <a id="19875" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19847" class="Function">psPllA</a> <a id="19882" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19884" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4632" class="InductiveConstructor">produ</a><a id="19889" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19890" class="Argument">𝓤</a> <a id="19892" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19894" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19895" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19403" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a><a id="19898" class="Symbol">)}{</a><a id="19901" class="Argument">𝓦</a> <a id="19903" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19905" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19906" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19403" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a><a id="19909" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="19912" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19762" class="Function">psllA</a>

   <a id="19922" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19922" class="Function">llA≅A</a> <a id="19928" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19930" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="19932" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19932" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="19934" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19936" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19937" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19593" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="19941" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19932" class="Bound">i</a><a id="19942" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19944" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#861" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="19946" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19947" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18234" class="Function">𝔄</a> <a id="19949" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19932" class="Bound">i</a><a id="19950" class="Symbol">)</a>
   <a id="19955" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19922" class="Function">llA≅A</a> <a id="19961" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19961" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="19963" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19965" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3811" class="Function">Trans-≅</a> <a id="19973" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19974" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19593" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="19978" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19961" class="Bound">i</a><a id="19979" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19981" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19982" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18234" class="Function">𝔄</a> <a id="19984" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19961" class="Bound">i</a><a id="19985" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19987" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19988" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2380" class="Function">sym-≅</a> <a id="19994" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4327" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="20004" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20006" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20007" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2380" class="Function">sym-≅</a> <a id="20013" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4327" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="20023" class="Symbol">)</a>

 <a id="20027" class="Comment">-- So, since PS⊆SP, we see that that the product of all subalgebras of a class 𝒦 belongs to SP(𝒦).</a>
 <a id="class-product-inclusions.class-prod-s-∈-sp"></a><a id="20127" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20127" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-sp</a> <a id="20145" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20147" href="MGS-FunExt-from-Univalence.html#2235" class="Function">hfunext</a><a id="20154" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20155" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19403" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a><a id="20158" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="20160" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19403" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a><a id="20163" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20165" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20167" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18408" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="20181" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20182" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3542" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="20184" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19331" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="20185" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20187" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="20189" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3542" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="20190" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20191" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4330" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="20193" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19331" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="20194" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="20197" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20127" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-sp</a> <a id="20215" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20215" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="20219" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20221" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14675" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a><a id="20226" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20227" class="Argument">hfe</a> <a id="20231" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20233" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20215" class="Bound">hfe</a><a id="20236" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20238" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19432" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a>
